	}
}

// The Monsters
ACTOR ShotgunCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastMediumTotalGib replaces ShotgunCat
{
	Game Doom
	Health 15
    Damage 1
	Radius 20
	Height 40
	Mass 20
    Speed 10
    Scale 0.8
	PainChance 170
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
    SeeSound "CATSIGHT"
	AttackSound "shotguy/attack"
	PainSound "CATPAIN"
	DeathSound "CATDIE"
    DropItem "SamsaraAmmo1Small_ROTWB", 125, 5
	Tag "Shotgun Cat"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Obituary "You were perforated by the bullets of the shotgun cat!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SPOS A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SPOS BB 3 A_Chase
        SPOS BB 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN3")
        SPOS DD 3 A_Chase
        SPOS DD 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN4")
        SPOS CC 3 A_Chase
        SPOS CC 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN3")
        SPOS DD 3 A_Chase
        SPOS DD 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN4")
		Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		SPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		SPOS F 10 A_CustomBulletAttack(5, 0, 1, 3, "BulletPuff")
		SPOS E 10
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SPOS G 2 A_Pain
		SPOS G 2
		Goto See
	Pain.MightyBoot:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        SPOS G 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
        SPOS G 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Death:
 		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SPOS I 4 A_Scream
		SPOS J 4 A_NoBlocking
        SPOS K 4
		SPOS L 4
        SPOS M 4
		SPOS H -1
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		SPOS G 2
		Loop
    Raise:
        SPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		SPOS H 1
        SPOS M 4
        SPOS L 4
        SPOS K 4
        SPOS J 4
        SPOS I 4
        Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		SPOS G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		SPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		SPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
	ExpanderLoopCoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
    }
}

actor ShotgunCat_Samsara_Shrink : ShotgunCat_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			SPOS G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SPOS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			SPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ShotgunCat_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:

			Goto Squish
	}

ACTOR DemonCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastLargeTotalGib replaces DemonCat
{
	Health 150
	PainChance 180
	Speed 18
	Radius 20
	Height 60
    Scale 0.7
	Mass 40
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP +FASTER +FASTMELEE
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
    SeeSound "RAWR"
	AttackSound "SWOOSH"
	DeathSound "GROUND"
    PainSound "RAWR2"
	Tag "Berserker Kitty"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Obituary "You were killed by a berserker kitty!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SARG A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		SARG AA 3 A_Chase
        SARG BB 3 A_Chase
        SARG A 0 A_PlaySound("STAMPF1")
        SARG AA 3 A_Chase
        SARG CC 3 A_Chase
        SARG A 0 A_PlaySound("STAMPF2")
        Loop
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
        SARG H 2 A_FaceTarget
        SARG H 2 A_PlaySound("SWOOSH")
        SARG I 3 A_SkelFist
        SARG J 3 A_FaceTarget
        SARG H 7 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Pain:
		SARG F 4 A_Pain
		Goto See
    Pain.MightyBoot:
        TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
        SARG F 2 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
        SARG F 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		SARG F 5
		SARG H 3
        SARG K 3
        SARG G 0 A_NoBlocking
        SARG G 0 A_Scream
        SARG G 5 Radius_Quake(1,10,0,10,0)
		SARG G -1
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		SARG F 2
		Loop
	Raise:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		SARG K 4
		SARG H 4
		SARG F 4
		Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
	Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		SARG F 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DemonCat_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoop
	ExpanderLoop:
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop
	ExpanderPop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		SARG A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
		Goto ExpanderLoopCoop

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}
}

{

	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0

	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0

			SARG F 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SARG AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:

		DukeStomp:

	}

ACTOR ChaingunCat_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastMediumTotalGib replaces ChaingunCat
{
	Game Doom
	Health 45
	Radius 20
	Height 40
	Mass 20
	Speed 5
    Scale 0.8
	PainChance 170
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTGIB
    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	SeeSound "CHAINCATSIGHT"
	PainSound "PUNCH8"
	DeathSound "CHAINCATDIE"
	AttackSound "chainguy/attack"
    DropItem "SamsaraAmmo2Small_ROTWB", 125, 2
	Tag "Chaingun Cat"
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Obituary "You were killed by the chaingun cat!"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		CPOS A 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		CPOS BB 3 A_Chase
        CPOS BB 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN3")
        CPOS DD 3 A_Chase
        CPOS DD 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN4")
        CPOS CC 3 A_Chase
        CPOS CC 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN3")
        CPOS DD 3 A_Chase
        CPOS DD 0 A_PlaySound("PASPLAN4")
        Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		CPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
		CPOS FE 4 BRIGHT A_CPosAttack
		CPOS F 1 A_CPosRefire
		Goto Missile+2
	Pain:
		CPOS G 2 A_Pain
		CPOS G 2
		Goto See
    Pain.MightyBoot:

        CPOS G 16 A_Pain
        Goto See
	Death:

		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
		CPOS I 4 A_Scream
		CPOS J 4 A_NoBlocking
        CPOS K 4
		CPOS L 4
        CPOS M 4
        CPOS H -1
		Stop
	Death.PainkillerStake:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	StakeDeath:
		CPOS G 2
		Loop
	Raise:
        CPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		CPOS H 1
        CPOS M 4
		CPOS L 4
        CPOS K 4
        CPOS J 4
        CPOS I 4
		Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.3,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.4,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.5,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.6,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.7,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.8,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.9,0)
		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(1,0)
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetShootable
		Goto See
    Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
		CPOS G 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChaingunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChaingunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChaingunCat_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

		"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ChaingunCat_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
		TNT1 A 2
		TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
		stop
	Death.ExpanderDMG:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
		CPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")

		"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
		loop

		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
	XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		CPOS A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
		loop
	ExpanderPopCoop:	
		"####" "#" 10
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
		TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
	    TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
        TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
		TNT1 A 1
		Stop
	}

actor ChaingunCat_Samsara_Shrink : ChaingunCat_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS

	MaxDropOffHeight 0

	Height 8
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0

	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0

			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)

			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			CPOS G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			CPOS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:

		Stop

		Loop

        TROO A 0
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyZorched",1,"ZorchRaise")
		TROO L 3
        TROO K 3
        TROO J 4
        TROO I 5
        Goto See
	ZorchRaise:
		"####" "#" 1 A_UnsetShootable
		"####" "#" 1 A_SpawnItem("SpawnFire2")
		"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("archvile/resummon")
		"####" "#" 1 A_TakeInventory("EnemyZorched",1)

		"####" "#" 3 A_SetTranslucent(0.2,0)

		BKAM D 5 bright
		BKAM E 0 A_PlaySound ("PUPPETHIT")
		BKAM E 5 A_NoBlocking

actor Beastling_Samsara_Shrink : Beastling_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS

	Height 8

	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			SARG H 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SARG AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG A 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG B 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG B 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG C 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG C 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG D 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SARG D 2 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Beastling_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

actor Follower_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium replaces ShotgunGuy
{
	scale .33
	health 60
	radius 10
	height 56
	mass 75
	speed 8
	painchance 170
	seesound "shotgun/sight"
	painsound "shotguy/pain"
	deathsound "shotguy/death"
	activesound "shotguy/active"
	dropitem "ShotgunDropHarmony"
	MONSTER
	BloodColor "ff 40 00"
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.15
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Pistol", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DukePistol", 1.1
	DamageFactor "ZorchPistol", 1.1
	DamageFactor "MarathonPistol", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Zorch", 1.1
	DamageFactor "Normal", 1.1
    DamageFactor "Disintegrate", 1.1
    DamageFactor "DukeDamage", 1.1
    DamageFactor "DukeIce", 1.1
	DamageFactor "MightyBoot", 1.5
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 255
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Follower"
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			SPOS AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			SPOS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Pain:
			SPOS G 3
			SPOS G 3 A_Pain
			goto See
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			SPOS G 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
			SPOS G 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.Shock:
		Pain.Tesla:
			CBGS A 4 A_Pain
			CBGS A 4
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"See")
			wait
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			SPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
			SPOS F 10 bright A_SPosAttack
			SPOS E 10
			goto See
		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			SPOS H 7
			SPOS I 7 A_Scream
			SPOS J 6 A_Fall
			SPOS KL 5
			VILE Z -1
			stop
		Death.DukeExplosive:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-3,"DukeGibStart")		
		Death.DukeDamage:
		Death.DukePistol:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeKillTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		Death.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		DukeGibStart:
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGib_ColorSpawner_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,"XDeath")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"XDeath")
			wait
		Death.CalebFire:
		Death.LifeLeech:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218, 2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("CalebDMTaunt1", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodBurningCorpse_Generic_Duke", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
			stop
		Death.PainkillerStake:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
			TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		StakeDeath:
			SPOS G 2
			Loop
		XDeath:
		    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			SPOS M 5
			SPOS N 5 A_XScream
			SPOS O 5 A_Fall
			SPOS PQRST 5
			SPOS U -1
			stop
		Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
			SPOS H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Follower_Samsara_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 2
			TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Death.ExpanderDMG:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			SPOS A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner_Duke", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			SPOS A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner_Duke", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

			Goto See

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)

			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

actor FallingFollower_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium replaces Archvile
{
	scale .30
	health 60
	speed 8
	radius 20
	height 56
	reactiontime 8
	painchance 170
	mass 75
	seesound "shotguy/sight"
	attacksound "shotguy/attack"
	painsound "shotguy/pain"
	deathsound "shotguy/raise"
	activesound "shotgun/active"
	MONSTER
	BloodColor "ff 40 00"
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.15
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Pistol", 1.1
	DamageFactor "DukePistol", 1.1
	DamageFactor "ZorchPistol", 1.1
	DamageFactor "MarathonPistol", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Zorch", 1.1
	DamageFactor "Normal", 1.1
    DamageFactor "Disintegrate", 1.1
    DamageFactor "DukeDamage", 1.1
    DamageFactor "DukeIce", 1.1
	DamageFactor "MightyBoot", 1.5
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 255
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Follower"
	+NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NOTARGET
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			FCAN A 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			FCAN B 2 A_Chase
			FCAN B 1 A_Chase
			FCAN C 2 A_Chase
			FCAN C 1 A_Chase
			BON1 A 2 A_Chase
			BON1 A 1 A_Chase
			BON1 B 2 A_Chase
			BON1 B 1 A_Chase
			BON1 C 2 A_Chase
			BON1 CC 6 A_Chase
			BON1 D 2 A_Chase
			BON1 D 6 A_Chase
		See2:
			SPOS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Pain:
			SPOS G 3
			SPOS G 3 A_Pain
			goto See2
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			SPOS G 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
			SPOS G 16 A_Pain
			Goto See2
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			SPOS E 10 A_FaceTarget
			SPOS F 10 bright A_SPosAttack
			SPOS E 10
			goto See2
		Pain.Shock:
		Pain.Tesla:
			CBGS A 4 A_Pain
			CBGS A 4
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"See")
			wait
		Death:
		    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			VILE R 5 A_XScream
			VILE S 5 A_Fall
			VILE TUVWX 5
			VILE Y -1
			stop
		Death.DukeExplosive:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-3,"DukeGibStart")		
		Death.DukeDamage:
		Death.DukePistol:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeKillTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		Death.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		DukeGibStart:
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGib_ColorSpawner_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,"XDeath")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"XDeath")
			wait
		Death.CalebFire:
		Death.LifeLeech:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218, 2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("CalebDMTaunt1", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodBurningCorpse_Generic_Duke", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
			stop
		Death.PainkillerStake:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
			TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		StakeDeath:
			SPOS G 2
			Loop
		XDeath:
		    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			SPOS M 5
			SPOS N 5 A_XScream
			SPOS O 5 A_Fall
			SPOS PQRST 5
			SPOS U -1
			stop
		Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
			SPOS H 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FallingFollower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FallingFollower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FallingFollower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FallingFollower_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			SPOS A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner_Duke", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}

actor FallingFollower_Samsara_Shrink : FallingFollower_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			SPOS G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			SPOS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)

			SPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			SPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("FallingFollower_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

actor WalkingCentaur_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterBeastLargeTotalGib replaces Revenant
{
	scale 0.30
	health 300
	speed 10
	radius 20
	height 56
	reactiontime 8
	painchance 100
	mass 500
	seesound "skeleton/sight"
	painsound "cyber/hoof"
	deathsound "skeleton/death"
	MONSTER
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.15
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	PainChance "MightyBoot", 255
	BloodColor "ff 40 00"
	+FLOORCLIP
	+LONGMELEERANGE
	+MISSILEMORE
	+NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Centuar"
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			CYBR AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			CYBR AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Pain:
			CYBR G 10 A_Pain
			goto See
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			CYBR G 2 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(12)
			CYBR G 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Missile:
		Melee:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			SKEL G 10 A_FaceTarget
			SKEL H 10 bright A_FaceTarget
			SKEL I 10 bright A_SkelMissile
			SKEL G 10 A_FaceTarget
			goto See
		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			CYBR H 5
			CYBR I 5 A_Scream
			CYBR JKL 5
			CYBR M -1 A_Fall
			stop
		Death.DukeExplosive:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-3,"DukeGibStart")		
		Death.DukeDamage:
		Death.DukePistol:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(218,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeKillTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		Death.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		DukeGibStart:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGib_ColorSpawner_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96, 2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraBossDeathToggler")
			TNT1 A 5
			Stop
		Death.PainkillerStake:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Painkiller_MonsterKill")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Painkiller_IsItGibbed")==1,"PainkillerGib")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Painkiller_RunStake",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Scream
			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
			TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		StakeDeath:
			CYBR G 2
			Loop
		Pain.ShrinkerDMG:
			CYBR G 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_NoBlocking
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/shrink")
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WalkingCentaur_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WalkingCentaur_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WalkingCentaur_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WalkingCentaur_Samsara_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			CYBR A 0

			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner_Duke", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}

		See:

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))

		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)

			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}

actor Soldier_Samsara : SamsaraMonsterHumanoidMedium replaces ChaingunGuy
{
	scale 0.30
	health 150
	speed 8
	radius 20
	height 56
	reactiontime 8
	painchance 170
	mass 100
	seesound "imp/sight"
	painsound "vile/pain"
	attacksound "chainguy/attack"
	deathsound "chainguy/death"
	activesound "chainguy/active"
	dropitem "ChingunDropHarmony"
	MONSTER
	var int user_scalex;
	var int user_scaley;
	Tag "Soldier"
	BloodColor "ff 40 00"
	DamageFactor "CorvusCrossbow", 1.15
	DamageFactor "DragonClaw", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Pistol", 1.25
	DamageFactor "DukePistol", 1.25
	DamageFactor "ZorchPistol", 1.25
	DamageFactor "MarathonPistol", 0.85
	DamageFactor "Zorch", 1.25

    DamageFactor "Fire", 1.15
    DamageFactor "Ice", 1.15

    +NOTDMATCH
    +NOICEDEATH

		Spawn:
			CPOS AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			CPOS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Missile:

		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			CPOS J 5 A_Fall
			CPOS K 5
			CPOS L -1
			stop
		Death.DukeExplosive:
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-3,"DukeGibStart")

		Death.DukePistol:

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeKillTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		Death.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Death")
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A -1 A_Jump(256,"Death")
			wait
		DukeGibStart:
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGib_ColorSpawner_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)

		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			CPOS A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner_Duke", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			CPOS A 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner_Duke", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}
}

actor Soldier_Samsara_Shrink : Soldier_Samsara
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ShrinkDMG", 0.0
	PainChance "ExpanderDMG", 0
	DamageFactor "ExpanderDMG", 0.0
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ShrunkToken",1,"SpawnLoop")
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale(scalex*0.2,scaley*0.2) // setting the scale in ACS does work, but the actor shows up at normal size for a split second
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_Shrinker", 0, 1)
			CPOS G 10
			Goto See
		SpawnLoop:
			CPOS AB 10 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS A 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS B 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS C 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeClass", 1, 3)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")
			CPOS D 3 A_Chase("","")
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(CallACS("Samsara_Shrinker", 3) == 0, "Forget")
			Loop
		Forget:
			"####" "#" 0 A_ClearTarget
			Goto See
		Grow:
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.35*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.35*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.4*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.4*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.45*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.45*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.65*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.65*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.75*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.75*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.8*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.8*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.85*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.85*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.9*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.9*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.95*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.95*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.0*(user_scalex/65536.0),1.0*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Soldier_Samsara", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToChildren("ShrunkPropertyTransfer",1)
			TNT1 A 2 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Squish:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("SquishToken", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("DukeStomp", 1, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 2 
			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256,3)
			"####" "#" 0 
			"####" "#" 2 A_Die("Squish")
			"####" "#" 0
			loop
		Death:
		XDeath:
		Death.Squish:
		XDeath.Squish:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeBootTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/enemygib", CHAN_BODY)
			TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeBloodPool_Duke",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			stop
		DukeStomp:
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeStomp", 1)
			Goto Squish
	}
}

actor Unknown1_Samsara replaces DoomImp
{
	health 60
	speed 8
	radius 20
	height 56
	reactiontime 8
	painchance 200
	mass 100
	seesound "imp/sight"
	painsound "imp/pain"
	deathsound "imp/death"
	MONSTER
	+FLOORCLIP
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			TROO AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			TROO AABBCC 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Pain:
			TROO G 1 bright
			loop
		Melee:
		Missile:
			TROO E 8 A_FaceTarget
			TROO F 8 A_SargAttack
		See2:
			BOSS AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Death:
			TROO I 8
			TROO J 8 A_Scream
			TROO K 6
			TROO L 6 A_Fall
			TROO M -1
			stop
		XDeath:
			TROO N 5
			TROO O 5 A_XScream
			TROO P 5
			TROO Q 5 A_Fall
			TROO RST 5
			TROO U -1
			stop
		Raise:
			TROO ML 8
			TROO KJI 6
			goto See
	}
}
